return false" target="morph">τῶν</a> <a href="morph?l=o%29mma%2Ftwn&amp;la=greek&amp;can=o%29mma%2Ftwn0&amp;prior=tw=n" onclick="m(this,1,0); return false" target="morph">ὀμμάτων</a></span> eye-<i>balls</i>, <i><span class="en">Arist.<u>Pr.</u>958a7</span></i>. </div><div class="lex_sense lex_sense3"><b>6.</b> <span class="greek"><a href="morph?l=s&amp;la=greek&amp;can=s10&amp;prior=o)mma/twn" onclick="m(this,11,0); return false" target="morph">ς</a>. <a href="morph?l=qala%2Fttiai&amp;la=greek&amp;can=qala%2Fttiai0&amp;prior=s" onclick="m(this,1,0); return false" target="morph">θαλάττιαι</a></span> sea-<i>balls</i>, <i><span class="en">Id.<u>HA</u>616a20</span></i>, <i><span class="en">Crito</span></i> ap.<i><span class="en">Gal.12.437</span></i>. </div><div class="lex_sense lex_sense3"><b>7.</b> <i>pill</i>, <i><span class="en">Archig.</span></i> ap. <i><span class="en">Orib.8.2.18</span></i>. </div><div class="lex_sense lex_sense3"><b>8.</b> <span class="greek"><a href="morph?l=plata%2Fnou&amp;la=greek&amp;can=plata%2Fnou0&amp;prior=qala/ttiai" onclick="m(this,1,0); return false" target="morph">πλατάνου</a> <a href="morph?l=sfai%3Drai&amp;la=greek&amp;can=sfai%3Drai0&amp;prior=plata/nou" onclick="m(this,1,0); return false" target="morph">σφαῖραι</a></span>, i.e. globular catkins, <i><span class="en">Dsc.4.73</span></i>. </div><div class="lex_sense lex_sense3"><b>9.</b> as a quantitative measure, “<span class="greek"><a href="morph?l=e%29pi%2Fbale&amp;la=greek&amp;can=e%29pi%2Fbale0&amp;prior=sfai=rai" onclick="m(this,1,0); return false" target="morph">ἐπίβαλε</a> . . <a href="morph?l=fu%2Fkous&amp;la=greek&amp;can=fu%2Fkous0&amp;prior=e)pi/bale" onclick="m(this,1,0); return false" target="morph">φύκους</a> <a href="morph?l=stupthri%2Fou&amp;la=greek&amp;can=stupthri%2Fou0&amp;prior=fu/kous" onclick="m(this,1,0); return false" target="morph">στυπτηρίου</a> <a href="morph?l=w%28s&amp;la=greek&amp;can=w%28s0&amp;prior=stupthri/ou" onclick="m(this,1,0); return false" target="morph">ὡς</a> <a href="morph?l=sfai%3Dran&amp;la=greek&amp;can=sfai%3Dran3&amp;prior=w(s" onclick="m(this,4,0); return false" target="morph">σφαῖραν</a></span>”  <i><span class="en"><u>PHolm.</u>16.32</span></i>.</div> </div><div class="footnotes en"> </div></div>	    </div> 	    <div id="text_footer">		<div id="text_desc">					Henry George Liddell.
